Local Open Scope cat.

Section Creates_Limits.

Definition creates_limit
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {J : graph}
  (F : diagram J (total_category D))
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)) : UU
:=
  ∑ (CC :
      ( ∑ (d : D (lim L))
          (δ : ∏ j : vertex J, d -->[limOut L j] (pr2 (dob F j))),
          forms_cone (c := (lim L ,, d)) F (λ j, (limOut L j ,, δ j))))
  , isLimCone _ _ (make_cone _ (pr2 (pr2 CC))).

Definition make_creates_limit
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {J : graph}
  {F : diagram J (total_category D)}
  {L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)}
  (d : D (lim L))
  (δ : ∏ j : vertex J, d -->[limOut L j] (pr2 (dob F j)))
  (Hcone : forms_cone (c := (lim L ,, d)) F (λ j, (limOut L j ,, δ j)))
  (Hlim : isLimCone _ _ (make_cone _ Hcone))
  : creates_limit F L
  := ((d ,, δ ,, Hcone) ,, Hlim).

Definition creates_limit_unique
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {J : graph}
  (F : diagram J (total_category D))
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)) : UU
:=
  ∑ (CC :
      ( ∃! (d : D (lim L))
          (δ : ∏ j : vertex J, d -->[limOut L j] (pr2 (dob F j))),
          forms_cone (c := (lim L ,, d)) F (λ j, (limOut L j ,, δ j))))
  , isLimCone _ _ (make_cone _ (pr2 (pr2 (pr1 CC)))).


C: category
D: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
CC: creates_limit F L
Hunique: ∏ (d : D (lim L))
(δ : ∏ j : vertex J,
     d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j))
(H : forms_cone F
       (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, δ j)),
d,, δ,, H = pr1 CC
creates_limit_unique F L


C: category
D: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
CC: creates_limit F L
Hunique: ∏ (d : D (lim L))
(δ : ∏ j : vertex J,
     d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j))
(H : forms_cone F
       (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, δ j)),
d,, δ,, H = pr1 CC
creates_limit_unique F L

  
C: category
D: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
CC: creates_limit F L
Hunique: ∏ (d : D (lim L))
(δ : ∏ j : vertex J,
     d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j))
(H : forms_cone F
       (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, δ j)),
d,, δ,, H = pr1 CC
∏
t : ∑ (d : D (lim L))
    (δ : ∏ j : vertex J,
         d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j)),
    forms_cone F (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, δ j),
t = pr1 CC

  exact (λ _, Hunique _ _ _).
Defined.

Definition creates_limit_unique_to_creates_limit
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {J : graph}
  (F : diagram J (total_category D))
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F))
  : creates_limit_unique F L → creates_limit F L
  := λ CC, (pr11 CC ,, pr2 CC).


C: category
P: C → UU
H: ∏ x y : C, P x → P y → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU
Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), isaprop (H x y a b f)
Hid: ∏ (x : C) (a : P x), H x x a a (identity x)
Hcomp: ∏ (x y z : C) (a : P x) 
(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)
D:= disp_struct C P H Hprop Hid Hcomp: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
d: D (lim L)
cone: ∏ j : vertex J,
d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j)
is_limit: ∏ (d' : total_category D)
(cone_out : ∏ u : vertex J,
            total_category D ⟦ d', 
            dob F u ⟧)
(is_cone : ∏ (u v : vertex J)
           (e : edge u v),
           cone_out u · dmor F e =
           cone_out v),
let L_lim_arrow :=
  limArrow L (pr1 d')
    (make_cone
       (λ u : vertex J, pr1 (cone_out u))
       (λ (u v : vertex J) 
        (e : edge u v),
        maponpaths pr1 (is_cone u v e))) in
pr2 d' -->[ L_lim_arrow] d
creates_limit F L

C: category
P: C → UU
H: ∏ x y : C, P x → P y → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU
Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), isaprop (H x y a b f)
Hid: ∏ (x : C) (a : P x), H x x a a (identity x)
Hcomp: ∏ (x y z : C) (a : P x) 
(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)

L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
d: D (lim L)
cone: ∏ j : vertex J,
d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j)
is_limit: ∏ (d' : total_category D)
(cone_out : ∏ u : vertex J,
            total_category D ⟦ d', 
            dob F u ⟧)
(is_cone : ∏ (u v : vertex J)
           (e : edge u v),
           cone_out u · dmor F e =
           cone_out v),

  limArrow L (pr1 d')
    (make_cone
       (λ u : vertex J, pr1 (cone_out u))
       (λ (u v : vertex J) 
        (e : edge u v),
        maponpaths pr1 (is_cone u v e))) in
pr2 d' -->[ L_lim_arrow] d
forms_cone F (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, cone j)
 abstract (
      do 3 intro;
      apply (subtypePairEquality (λ _, Hprop _ _ _ _ _));
      apply (limOutCommutes L)
    ).

C: category
P: C → UU
H: ∏ x y : C, P x → P y → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU
Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)

(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)

            total_category D ⟦ d',

cone': Graphs.Limits.cone F d'
(λ x : total_category D ⟦ d', lim L,, d ⟧,
 is_cone_mor cone'
   (make_cone (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, cone j)
      (creates_limit_disp_struct_subproof C P H Hprop
         Hid Hcomp J F L d cone)) x)
  (limArrow L (pr1 d')
     (make_cone (λ u : vertex J, pr1 (pr1 cone' u))

      intro u;
      apply (subtypePairEquality (λ _, Hprop _ _ _ _ _));

C: category
P: C → UU
H: ∏ x y : C, P x → P y → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU
Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), isaprop (H x y a b f)
Hid: ∏ (x : C) (a : P x), H x x a a (identity x)
Hcomp: ∏ (x y z : C) (a : P x) 
(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)
D:= disp_struct C P H Hprop Hid Hcomp: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
d: D (lim L)
cone: ∏ j : vertex J,
d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j)
is_limit: ∏ (d' : total_category D)
(cone_out : ∏ u : vertex J,
            total_category D ⟦ d', 
            dob F u ⟧)
(is_cone : ∏ (u v : vertex J)
           (e : edge u v),
           cone_out u · dmor F e =
           cone_out v),
let L_lim_arrow :=
  limArrow L (pr1 d')
    (make_cone
       (λ u : vertex J, pr1 (cone_out u))
       (λ (u v : vertex J) 
        (e : edge u v),
        maponpaths pr1 (is_cone u v e))) in
pr2 d' -->[ L_lim_arrow] d
d': total_category D
cone': Graphs.Limits.cone F d'
(λ cntr : ∑ x : total_category D ⟦ d', lim L,, d ⟧,
          is_cone_mor cone'
            (make_cone
               (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, cone j)
               (creates_limit_disp_struct_subproof C P
                  H Hprop Hid Hcomp J F L d cone)) x,
 ∏
 t : ∑ x : total_category D ⟦ d', lim L,, d ⟧,
     is_cone_mor cone'
       (make_cone
          (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, cone j)
          (creates_limit_disp_struct_subproof C P H
             Hprop Hid Hcomp J F L d cone)) x,
 t = cntr)
  ((limArrow L (pr1 d')
      (make_cone (λ u : vertex J, pr1 (pr1 cone' u))
         (λ (u v : vertex J) (e : edge u v),
          maponpaths pr1 (pr2 cone' u v e))),,
    is_limit d' (pr1 cone') (pr2 cone')),,
   creates_limit_disp_struct_subproof0 C P H Hprop Hid
     Hcomp J F L d cone is_limit d' cone')
 abstract (
      intro t;
      repeat apply subtypePairEquality;
      [ intro;
        apply impred_isaprop;
        intro;
        apply (homset_property (total_category _))
      | simpl;
        intro;
        apply Hprop
      | apply (limArrowUnique L);
        intro;
        exact (maponpaths pr1 (pr2 t u)) ]
    ).
Defined.


C: category
P: C → UU
H: ∏ x y : C, P x → P y → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU
Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), isaprop (H x y a b f)
Hid: ∏ (x : C) (a : P x), H x x a a (identity x)
Hcomp: ∏ (x y z : C) (a : P x) 
(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)
D:= disp_struct C P H Hprop Hid Hcomp: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
CC: creates_limit F L
d_is_unique: ∏ d' : pr1 D (lim L),
(∏ j : vertex J,
 d' -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j))
→ d' = pr11 CC
creates_limit_unique F L

Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), isaprop (H x y a b f)
Hid: ∏ (x : C) (a : P x), H x x a a (identity x)
Hcomp: ∏ (x y z : C) (a : P x) 
(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)
D:= disp_struct C P H Hprop Hid Hcomp: disp_cat C

C: category
P: C → UU
H: ∏ x y : C, P x → P y → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU
Hprop: ∏ (x y : C) (a : P x) (b : P y)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), isaprop (H x y a b f)
Hid: ∏ (x : C) (a : P x), H x x a a (identity x)
Hcomp: ∏ (x y z : C) (a : P x) 
(b : P y) (c : P z) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
H x y a b f → H y z b c g → H x z a c (f · g)
D:= disp_struct C P H Hprop Hid Hcomp: disp_cat C
J: graph
F: diagram J (total_category D)
L: LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F)
CC: creates_limit F L
d_is_unique: ∏ d' : pr1 D (lim L),
(∏ j : vertex J,
 d' -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j))
→ d' = pr11 CC
∏ (d : D (lim L))
(δ : ∏ j : vertex J, d -->[ limOut L j] pr2 (dob F j))
(H : forms_cone F (λ j : vertex J, limOut L j,, δ j)),
d,, δ,, H = pr1 CC

  abstract (
    intros d δ H0;
    apply subtypePairEquality;
    [ intro;
      use (isaprop_total2 (_ ,, _) (λ _, _ ,, _));
        repeat (apply impred_isaprop; intro);
      [ apply Hprop
      | apply (homset_property (total_category _)) ]
    | exact (d_is_unique _ δ) ]
  ).
Defined.

  abstract (
    do 3 intro;
    apply subtypePairEquality';
    [ apply H
    | use (isaprop_total2 (_ ,, _) (λ _, _ ,, _));
      [ apply impred_isaprop;
        intro;
        apply isapropunit
      | do 3 (apply impred_isaprop; intro);
        simpl;
        apply isaset_dirprod;
        [ apply homset_property
        | apply isasetunit] ] ]

Definition creates_limits {C : category} (D : disp_cat C) : UU := ∏
  (J : graph)
  (F : diagram J (total_category D))
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F) ),
  creates_limit F L.

Definition creates_limits_unique {C : category} (D : disp_cat C) : UU := ∏
  (J : graph)
  (F : diagram J (total_category D))
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F) ),
  creates_limit_unique F L.

End Creates_Limits.

Definition total_limit
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {J : graph}
  {F : diagram J (total_category D)}
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category D) F))
  (H : creates_limit F L)
  : LimCone F
  := make_LimCone _ _ _ (pr2 H).

Definition total_limits
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {J : graph}
  (H : creates_limits D)
  (X : Lims_of_shape J C)
  : Lims_of_shape J (total_category D)
  := λ d, total_limit (X _) (H _ _ _).

Section fiber.

  Context {C : category}.
  Context {D : disp_cat C}.
  Context (c : C).
  Context {J : graph}.

  Context {F : diagram J (fiber_category D c)}.
  Context (L : LimCone (constant_diagram J c)).
  Context (H : creates_limit _ ((L : LimCone
    (mapdiagram (fiber_to_total_functor D c ∙ pr1_category D) F)
  ) : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category _) (mapdiagram _ F)))).

  Let Δ : C⟦c, lim L⟧
    := limArrow L _ (constant_cone J c).

  Let L' : LimCone (mapdiagram (fiber_to_total_functor D c) F)
    := make_LimCone _ _ _ (pr2 H).

  Context (candidate : cartesian_lift (pr11 H) Δ).

  Definition fiber_lim
    : D[{c}]
    := pr1 candidate.

  Definition fiber_lim_out
    (u : vertex J)
    : D[{c}] ⟦ fiber_lim , dob F u ⟧
    := (transportf _ (limArrowCommutes _ _ _ _) (pr12 candidate ;; pr121 H u)).

(* Check fiber_limit. *)

Definition fiber_limits
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  (c : C)
  {J : graph}
  (H : creates_limits D)
  (L : Lims_of_shape J C)
  (cl : cleaving D)
  : Lims_of_shape J (D[{c}])
  := λ F, fiber_limit c
    (L _)
    (H _ _ _)
    (cl _ _ _ _).

Section Sigma.
  Context {C : category}.
  Context {D : disp_cat C}.
  Context {E : disp_cat (total_category D)}.
  Context (D' := sigma_disp_cat E).
  Context {J : graph}.
  Context {d : diagram J (total_category D')}.
  Context {L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category _) d)}.

  Context (HD : creates_limit (mapdiagram (total_functor (sigmapr1_disp_functor E)) d) L).
  Context (HE : creates_limit (mapdiagram (sigma_to_E_total_functor E) d) (total_limit _ HD)).

  Definition tip_sigma_disp_cat
    : D' (lim L)
    := pr11 HD ,, pr11 HE.

  Definition cone_sigma_disp_cat
    (j : vertex J)
    : tip_sigma_disp_cat -->[limOut L j] pr2 (dob d j)
    := pr121 HD j ,, pr121 HE j.

  Section Arrow.

    Context (d' : total_category D').
    Context (d'_cone : cone d d').

    Let d_cone : LimCone (mapdiagram (sigma_to_E_total_functor E) d)
      := (make_LimCone _ _ _ (pr2 HE)).

    Let e_cone : cone (mapdiagram (sigma_to_E_total_functor E) d) (sigma_to_E_total_functor E d')
      := mapcone (sigma_to_E_total_functor E) _ d'_cone.

    Definition sigma_lim_arrow
      : total_category D'⟦d', lim L,, tip_sigma_disp_cat⟧
      := (# (E_to_sigma_total_functor E))%cat (limArrow d_cone _ e_cone).

End Sigma.

Definition creates_limits_sigma_disp_cat
  {C : category}
  {D : disp_cat C}
  {E : disp_cat (total_category D)}
  (D' := sigma_disp_cat E)
  {J : graph}
  (F : diagram J (total_category D'))
  (L : LimCone (mapdiagram (pr1_category _) F))
  (HD : creates_limit (mapdiagram (total_functor (sigmapr1_disp_functor E)) F) L)
  (HE : creates_limit (mapdiagram (sigma_to_E_total_functor E) F) (total_limit _ HD))
  : creates_limit F L
  := make_creates_limit
    (tip_sigma_disp_cat HD HE)
    (cone_sigma_disp_cat HD HE)
    (forms_cone_sigma_disp_cat HD HE)
    (is_lim_cone_sigma_disp_cat HD HE).
